  Actor Pipeline  (4 stages per step)
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    1. Quantum IRS selection
       State  : a_t ∈ R^17  =  5×(1+2)+2×1  (affinity ‖ D_k ‖ |g_SU|)
       Encoder: 17 → B2-DualAE → 16  (z_t)  [IRS:2D + User:2×5D→P]
       Decoder: 16 → 32 → 17  (AE regulariser)
       QC     : 16-dim → 8 qubits (H+U_enc+U_var×3+1×CZ-bridge) → 16-dim+1×ZZ-cross(B4)  (o_hat)
       Post-NN: 32 → 256 → 128 → 5×2 logits
       Output : φ ∈ {0,…,1}^5  (2^5 combinations)
    2. PhaseMLP  (IRS phase shifts — active IRS only)
       State  : c^SRU_m ∈ R^31 per active IRS  ([Re+Im c^SRU(10) ‖ z_t(16) ‖ phi_mask(5)])
       Net    : 31 → 64 → 128 → 256 → 128 → 96  (shared weights, N=24 elements/IRS, categorical)
       Output : phase_idx ∈ {0..3}^{G×24}  (G ≤ 1 active IRS, expanded to 1×24)
    3. PowerMLP  (power allocation)
       State  : h_eff+z_t ∈ R^26  ([Re+Im h_eff(10) ‖ z_t(16)])
       Net    : 26 → 64 → 128 → 64 → 7  softmax → ×P_S
       Output : w_c_vec ∈ R^{G+1}  (per-group common, G≤1),  w_p ∈ R^5  (private)  [Σ=P_S]
    4. CkMLP  (common-rate split)
       State  : [D_k, R_p_k, R_c_g_k, shortfall_k, phi_k] ∈ R^25  (per user)
       Net    : 25 → 64 → 128 → 64 → 32 → 5  within-group softmax → C_k
       Output : C_k ∈ R^5  (Σ_{k∈g} C_k = R_c_g per group)

  Critic  (State-Value MLP  V(s))
    Input        : s_t (17)  =  17 total
    Architecture : 17 → 512 → 256 → 128 → 64 → 1  (V)
